[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen processing a NetBIOS packet. According to the ASAN report:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-netbios.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m1144:16[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Operation**: READ of size [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Address**: `[0m[1;36m0x00000885eea8[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Affected Variable**: Global variable `dissect_netb` defined at line [0m[1;36m1016[0m[39m of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-netbios.c`, which has a size of [0m[1;36m264[0m[39m bytes[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Overflow**: The read occurs exactly at offset [0m[1;36m264[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after the end of the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Execution Context[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through the following call stack:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Fuzzer entry point: `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzzshark.c`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Packet dissection: `epan_dissect_run` → `dissect_record`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Frame dissection: `dissect_frame` in `packet-frame.c`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Post-dissectors: `call_all_postdissectors`[0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer was configured to test the `handler_netbios` target with the following [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mHexadecimal: `[0m[1;36m0x10[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0xef[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0xfa[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Layout Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe ASAN shadow bytes reveal:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter examining the code snippets and the evaluation report, I have identified the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause of the global-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs at line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m in `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c` where [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bounds check is incorrectly implemented:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_netb` array contains [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m function pointers with valid indices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, `[0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m, which is **not** a valid index. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen a malformed packet contains a command value >= [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlike [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m from the fuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe MIN operation clamps it to [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m, and the subsequent array access at line [0m[1;36m1144[0m[39m:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msession_id = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcommand[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, pinfo, offset, netb_tree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to read `dissect_netb[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m33[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which is one element past the end of the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray, causing an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read overflow.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Design Intent[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `dissect_netb` array is designed with:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Indices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x00[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x1f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Specific command handlers for known NetBIOS commands[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Index [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: A catch-all `dissect_netb_unknown` handler for any [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid/unknown commands[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe bounds check should clamp invalid command values to index [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe last valid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to use the unknown handler safely.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Supporting Evidence[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSimilar patterns in the Wireshark codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-lte-rrc.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrate the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect approach:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturn vals[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39midx, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvals[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis pattern is used consistently across multiple lookup functions to prevent [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer overflows while providing a safe fallback value.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Correct the Bounds Check[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c`, line [0m[1;36m1108[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current code**:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code**:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns [0m[1;36m33[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Valid array indices are [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m through [0m[1;36m32[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Subtracting [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m ensures the maximum clamped value is [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, which is the last valid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindex[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This preserves the design intent: any command value >= [0m[1;36m0x20[0m[39m will use the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_netb_unknown` handler at index [0m[1;36m32[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Apply the fix to line [0m[1;36m1108[0m[39m** in `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c`:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `[0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m[1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35marray_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdissect_netb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is a one-line change that requires modifying only the bounds check [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpression[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Verify the fix addresses the vulnerability**:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With the corrected bounds check, any command value from the packet [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill be clamped to a maximum of [0m[1;36m32[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The array access at line [0m[1;36m1144[0m[39m will always use a valid index [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer input [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand = [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be clamped to [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, invoking [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_netb_unknown` safely[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal change**: Only one line needs modification, reducing the risk of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new bugs[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves existing logic**: [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All valid NetBIOS commands [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0x00[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0x1f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to use their specific handlers[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invalid commands use the `dissect_netb_unknown` handler as originally intended[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to the dissector function signatures or array structure[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows established patterns**: The fix aligns with proven patterns used [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39melsewhere in the Wireshark codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-lte-rrc.c[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No side effects**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The switch statement at line [0m[1;36m1153[0m[39m continues to work correctly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mswitch [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatements don't cause buffer overflows[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `val_to_str_ext` call at line [0m[1;36m1111[0m[39m for displaying command names handles [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many value safely[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix doesn't affect any other dissector or component[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Addresses the exact issue**: The ASAN report shows the overflow occurs when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccessing index [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39marray_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and this fix prevents that specific access[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No negative side effects expected** because:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The last array element [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindex [0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is already `dissect_netb_unknown`, designed as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma catch-all handler[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any command value >= [0m[1;36m0x20[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now safely invoke this handler[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The behavior for valid commands [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Verification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix can be verified by:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Testing with the original fuzzer input that triggered the issue: [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`\[0m[1;36m020[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m357[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m372[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Confirming that command value [0m[1;36m0xff[0m[39m is clamped to [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m instead of [0m[1;36m33[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Verifying that `dissect_netb_unknown` is invoked without buffer overflow[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Running existing unit tests to ensure no regressions[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
